Join Cargill's global team of 155,000 employees who are committed to safe, responsible and sustainable ways to nourish the world. This position is in Cargill’s agricultural supply chain business, where we seamlessly connect farming customers with food, feed and industry.

JOB PURPOSE AND IMPACT

The Nutritionist - Feed will provide advice and insights to internal stakeholders and our feed mill customers, while helping the business achieve growth targets. The business supplies feed ingredients to feed producers and you will make relevant connections between raw materials, the feed mill and animal performance at farm level.

You will become the go-to person for feed ingredient know-how and nutrient evaluation related questions. Ingredients in the portfolio include raw materials like grains (corn, wheat) and vegetable protein sources (sunflower, rape, soya).

We seek a collaborative and knowledgeable team player, who has a thorough understanding of feed ingredients & animal nutrition and who will support new business development projects and customer enquiries.

KEY ACCOUNTABILITIES

Acts as an educated resource to both customers and internal stakeholders in the field of feed ingredient specifications and applications.
Collaborates with commercial teams on providing product, application, ingredient, processing expertise and training.
Acts as the technical link between commercial teams and R&D function and assesses opportunities for improvement and provide advice and consultation.
Understand customers’ needs and help them to improve their business and animal performance at farm level, through our product solutions and services.
Support cross functional teams by compiling and analyzing data for projects.
Other duties as assigned.

MINIMUM QUALIFICATIONS

Bachelor’s degree in a related field of agriculture, animal science, nutrition or business
Fluent in English

PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS

Experience in compound feed industry and connections in animal nutrition research institutes.

Our Offer

In return for your expertise and commitment, we will provide a fast paced stimulating international environment, which will stretch your abilities and channel your talents. We also offer competitive salary and benefits combined with outstanding career development opportunities in one of the largest and most solid private companies in the world.

The Nutritionist - Feed will provide advice and insights to internal stakeholders and our feed mill customers, while helping the business achieve growth targets. The business supplies feed ingredients to feed producers and you will make relevant connections between raw materials, the feed mill and animal performance at farm level.

You will become the go-to person for feed ingredient know-how and nutrient evaluation related questions. Ingredients in the portfolio include raw materials like grains (corn, wheat) and vegetable protein sources (sunflower, rape, soya).

We seek a collaborative and knowledgeable team player, who has a thorough understanding of feed ingredients & animal nutrition and who will support new business development projects and customer enquiries.

KEY ACCOUNTABILITIES

Acts as an educated resource to both customers and internal stakeholders in the field of feed ingredient specifications and applications.
Collaborates with commercial teams on providing product, application, ingredient, processing expertise and training.
Acts as the technical link between commercial teams and R&D function and assesses opportunities for improvement and provide advice and consultation.
Understand customers’ needs and help them to improve their business and animal performance at farm level, through our product solutions and services.
Support cross functional teams by compiling and analyzing data for projects.
Other duties as assigned.

MINIMUM QUALIFICATIONS

Bachelor’s degree in a related field of agriculture, animal science, nutrition or business
Fluent in English

PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS

Experience in compound feed industry and connections in animal nutrition research institutes.

Our Offer

In return for your expertise and commitment, we will provide a fast paced stimulating international environment, which will stretch your abilities and channel your talents. We also offer competitive salary and benefits combined with outstanding career development opportunities in one of the largest and most solid private companies in the world.

Interested? Then make sure to send us your CV and cover letter in English today.

We seek a collaborative and knowledgeable team player, who has a thorough understanding of feed ingredients & animal nutrition and who will support new business development projects and customer enquiries.

KEY ACCOUNTABILITIES

Acts as an educated resource to both customers and internal stakeholders in the field of feed ingredient specifications and applications.
Collaborates with commercial teams on providing product, application, ingredient, processing expertise and training.
Acts as the technical link between commercial teams and R&D function and assesses opportunities for improvement and provide advice and consultation.
Understand customers’ needs and help them to improve their business and animal performance at farm level, through our product solutions and services.
Support cross functional teams by compiling and analyzing data for projects.
Other duties as assigned.

MINIMUM QUALIFICATIONS

Bachelor’s degree in a related field of agriculture, animal science, nutrition or business
Fluent in English

PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS

Experience in compound feed industry and connections in animal nutrition research institutes.

Our Offer

In return for your expertise and commitment, we will provide a fast paced stimulating international environment, which will stretch your abilities and channel your talents. We also offer competitive salary and benefits combined with outstanding career development opportunities in one of the largest and most solid private companies in the world.

29,supply,Indeed,p_d91842d6d2fb660f,Operations & Logistics Manager,Ace  Tate, Amsterdam,"Ace & Tate is a leading optical fashion brand with 70+ stores all across Europe and a global e-commerce site. As we are rapidly expanding throughout Europe (online and offline) and are working towards a seamless omnichannel experience, we are growing our Supply Chain team.
In the past years, we have focused on setting up our infrastructure, processes and systems in such a way that we have a solid set up to support the rapid growth of Ace & Tate. The next phase is to further optimize our network and infrastructure to deliver our product faster, have better insights in our flows and become more efficient in our geographic spread.
To help us continue the success of Ace & Tate, we are on the hunt for an experienced Operations & Logistics Manager to join us. Reporting into the Supply Chain Director you’ll be responsible for overseeing and optimising all the operations and logistics related flows, as well as managing our ambitious Operations & Logistics team. This position is full-time and immediately available.
Although we are working remotely at present, our headquarters are based in Amsterdam — so, when it’s possible to do so, we’d ideally like to work with you in person! Depending on COVID-19 measures, your onboarding will likely take place online.
You'll be...
Managing the Operation & Logistics team (5 direct reports).
Overseeing all processes, performance, and costs for running our Ace & Tate operations.
Defining and implementing the Operations & Logistics roadmap together with the internal stakeholders and implement the logistics changes or processes of the future.
Overseeing the warehouse/transportation/production budget and KPI's.
The project manager for logistics/infrastructure/transportation-related topics (such as geographical roll-out outside EU, designing and implementing the operations set up for new products).
Ensuring all flows of products flow through the existing warehouse & process set up.
Further professionalising and improving the 3PL and production partners' way of working and further roll out the MBR/QBR way of working.
Continuously seeking to optimise the processes and the network to get non-value-added activities out of our Operations and Supply Chain teams.
You...
Have a relevant Bachelor’s or Master’s degree, e.g. in logistics or business administration.
Have 6-8 years of logistics/operations experience, with 2-3 years experience in managing and developing team members.
Are good at conceptualising future-proof operations set up and processes and are able to facilitate complex process conversations.
Are experienced with continuous improvement of end-2-end processes (using methods like lean/six sigma, etc).
Have managed geographical expansion from a logistics point of view before and you are familiar with customs processes and documents, incoterms, etc.
Have experience in evaluating & redesigning the current network setup (including selection/tender management of our partners).
Are a go-getter which we can fully rely on to run and shape our growing operations network.
We offer you...
The chance to be part of a young and ambitious team.
Personal and professional development.
A broad scope of responsibilities and growth opportunities.
An international company with a fun, hard-working and dynamic atmosphere.
Healthy lunch, good coffee, all-day snacks, and Friday drinks — when we’re back at the office.
Frequent updates to your own eyewear collection!
Jeez, that was a lot. Still with us? If you are, and you’re thinking that you might just fit this profile, please apply via the form below. We’d love to hear from you.

38,supply,Indeed,pj_a3e4c8ddf4049d73,Nutritionist - Feed,Cargill, Schiphol,"Want to build a stronger, more sustainable future and cultivate your career? Join Cargill's global team of 155,000 employees who are committed to safe, responsible and sustainable ways to nourish the world. This position is in Cargill’s agricultural supply chain business, where we seamlessly connect farming customers with food, feed and industry.

JOB PURPOSE AND IMPACT

The Nutritionist - Feed will provide advice and insights to internal stakeholders and our feed mill customers, while helping the business achieve growth targets. The business supplies feed ingredients to feed producers and you will make relevant connections between raw materials, the feed mill and animal performance at farm level.

You will become the go-to person for feed ingredient know-how and nutrient evaluation related questions. Ingredients in the portfolio include raw materials like grains (corn, wheat) and vegetable protein sources (sunflower, rape, soya).

We seek a collaborative and knowledgeable team player, who has a thorough understanding of feed ingredients & animal nutrition and who will support new business development projects and customer enquiries.

KEY ACCOUNTABILITIES

Acts as an educated resource to both customers and internal stakeholders in the field of feed ingredient specifications and applications.
Collaborates with commercial teams on providing product, application, ingredient, processing expertise and training.
Acts as the technical link between commercial teams and R&D function and assesses opportunities for improvement and provide advice and consultation.
Understand customers’ needs and help them to improve their business and animal performance at farm level, through our product solutions and services.
Support cross functional teams by compiling and analyzing data for projects.
Other duties as assigned.

MINIMUM QUALIFICATIONS

Bachelor’s degree in a related field of agriculture, animal science, nutrition or business
Fluent in English

PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS

Experience in compound feed industry and connections in animal nutrition research institutes.

Our Offer

In return for your expertise and commitment, we will provide a fast paced stimulating international environment, which will stretch your abilities and channel your talents. We also offer competitive salary and benefits combined with outstanding career development opportunities in one of the largest and most solid private companies in the world.

Interested? Then make sure to send us your CV and cover letter in English today.

Follow us on LinkedIn: https://www.linkedin.com/company/cargill

Cargill is committed to being an inclusive employer. 40,supply,Indeed,p_500434d5d875370f,Nutritionist - Feed,Cargill, Schiphol,"Want to build a stronger, more sustainable future and cultivate your career? Join Cargill's global team of 155,000 employees who are committed to safe, responsible and sustainable ways to nourish the world. This position is in Cargill’s agricultural supply chain business, where we seamlessly connect farming customers with food, feed and industry.

JOB PURPOSE AND IMPACT

The Nutritionist - Feed will provide advice and insights to internal stakeholders and our feed mill customers, while helping the business achieve growth targets. The business supplies feed ingredients to feed producers and you will make relevant connections between raw materials, the feed mill and animal performance at farm level.

You will become the go-to person for feed ingredient know-how and nutrient evaluation related questions. Ingredients in the portfolio include raw materials like grains (corn, wheat) and vegetable protein sources (sunflower, rape, soya).

We seek a collaborative and knowledgeable team player, who has a thorough understanding of feed ingredients & animal nutrition and who will support new business development projects and customer enquiries.

KEY ACCOUNTABILITIES

Acts as an educated resource to both customers and internal stakeholders in the field of feed ingredient specifications and applications.
Collaborates with commercial teams on providing product, application, ingredient, processing expertise and training.
Acts as the technical link between commercial teams and R&D function and assesses opportunities for improvement and provide advice and consultation.
Understand customers’ needs and help them to improve their business and animal performance at farm level, through our product solutions and services.
Support cross functional teams by compiling and analyzing data for projects.
Other duties as assigned.

MINIMUM QUALIFICATIONS

Bachelor’s degree in a related field of agriculture, animal science, nutrition or business
Fluent in English

PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS

Experience in compound feed industry and connections in animal nutrition research institutes.

49,supply,Indeed,p_5e9689c8c5e08e04,Supply Chain Manager,Stora Enso, Amsterdam,"Can you help us take wooden buildings to new heights? Come join us!

We are looking for a Supply Chain Manager for our Amsterdam Unit in Wood Products Division. As a Supply Chain Manager, your job will be to lead all activities and staff within the Supply Chain department in the mill. You will secure efficient and well maintained warehousing and logistics with external suppliers. Based on demand plan from sales, you must source and manage the flow of The Amsterdam Unit, to secure delivery on time and further develop related processes to excellence. You will be the main contact point for the Supply Chain Organization in The Netherlands in regard to delivery performance development in the pipeline. Naturally you will be an expert in procurement for Amsterdam Unit in Wood Products and you will have responsibility for managing and sourcing the required services and assets in cooperation with the relevant departments. As a member of the mill management team, you will be part of the future growth and the overall safety of the unit.
Stora Enso is a leading global provider of renewable solutions in packaging, biomaterials, wooden constructions and paper. Come grow a renewable world. And you will grow too.

Your main tasks and responsibilities will be:
Manage DU purchasing process to meet the sales target; planning, execution and deviation management;maintain transparent communication with counter parties’ i.e. logistics and mills
Manage and source required raw and further processed material, assets and services to run the Amsterdam Unit in co-operation with The Mill Director. Ensure all major category spend (warehousing / transport / customs) are properly tendered and contracted with written contracts in place for all major vendors.
Responsible for inventory accuracy and stock write-off management
Responsible for overall stock take process
Support WP sales organization with accurate and timely information of customer deliveries and availability of products
Ensure compliancy to rules & legislation within responsibility area
Participate in business planning and target setting as a member of the management; execute within responsibility area
Jointly with Mill Director; further develop end-to-end supply chain processes in WP pipeline in terms of cost, efficiency, capital employed, delivery accuracy and availability.
Responsible for the Chain of Custody (CoC) process and other sustainability matters
What we Offer
With our values, “Lead and Do what’s right”, we endeavor to set an example in all aspects of our business as well as sustainability. We dare to take the initiative and constantly ask ourselves what more can we do, what can we do better. This is an excellent opportunity for you to be a part of the journey Stora Enso is on – transforming from a traditional forest industry company, into a renewable materials growth company – an industry with great potential driven by global megatrends. You will be working in an encouraging environment and we will provide you the help and training that you need. This role will give you an opportunity to grow as a professional and get to apply and broaden what you already know

Qualifications
In order to succeed in this role, you will have:
Relevant bachelor degree or equivalent, professional qualification in supply chain
Experience in S&OP process and tools is an advantage
Strong analytical skills together with a structured & systematic approach
Excellent communication skills and fluent in English and the willingness to learn Dutch
Comprehensive view with excellent analytical skills and persistence in order to get things done
Ability to cooperate, having a natural interest to involve people and support others
Performance oriented and ability to always deliver against set targets and deadlines

Manage and source required raw and further processed material, assets and services to run the Amsterdam Unit in co-operation with The Mill Director. Ensure all major category spend (warehousing / transport / customs) are properly tendered and contracted with written contracts in place for all major vendors.
Responsible for inventory accuracy and stock write-off management
Responsible for overall stock take process
Support WP sales organization with accurate and timely information of customer deliveries and availability of products
Ensure compliancy to rules & legislation within responsibility area
Participate in business planning and target setting as a member of the management; execute within responsibility area
Jointly with Mill Director; further develop end-to-end supply chain processes in WP pipeline in terms of cost, efficiency, capital employed, delivery accuracy and availability.
Responsible for the Chain of Custody (CoC) process and other sustainability matters
What we Offer
With our values, “Lead and Do what’s right”, we endeavor to set an example in all aspects of our business as well as sustainability. We dare to take the initiative and constantly ask ourselves what more can we do, what can we do better. This is an excellent opportunity for you to be a part of the journey Stora Enso is on – transforming from a traditional forest industry company, into a renewable materials growth company – an industry with great potential driven by global megatrends. You will be working in an encouraging environment and we will provide you the help and training that you need. This role will give you an opportunity to grow as a professional and get to apply and broaden what you already know

Qualifications
In order to succeed in this role, you will have:
Relevant bachelor degree or equivalent, professional qualification in supply chain
Experience in S&OP process and tools is an advantage
Strong analytical skills together with a structured & systematic approach
Excellent communication skills and fluent in English and the willingness to learn Dutch
Comprehensive view with excellent analytical skills and persistence in order to get things done
Ability to cooperate, having a natural interest to involve people and support others
Performance oriented and ability to always deliver against set targets and deadlines
3-5 years of experience in the purchasing of Wood Products
IT literate: fluent with MS excel and ERP’s on basic reporting working process level, previous experience on any advanced reporting and analytics tool on SC area is an advantage

64,supply,Indeed,p_b46cb3e2ecefa368,Process Improvement Project Coordinator,IDEXX, Hoofddorp,"Our Distribution and Instrument Service center is looking for a Process Improvement Project Coordinator to continue supporting the rapid growth of our organization. Seated in Hoofddorp (Amsterdam area), which is our international headquarter location, we are on the center stage of our operations in the EMEA and APO region. This is an outstanding opportunity to be part of our international operations team of a growing biotech company that was recently added to the S&P 500 and the NASDAQ 100 Index!
The purpose of this very versatile role is to support the Supply Chain operations team with the increasing volume of project-related work driven by the growth of the organization. You will participate in and / or lead small and large initiatives and projects. Depending on the situation, you will be responsible for either the organizational and planning aspects, or the execution, or both.
In this Role:
You will be supporting continuous improvement in the Supply Chain organization, analysing and evaluating processes, proactively coming up with improvement recommendations
You will be building a solid business case using a problem-solving method and data analysis and taking an active role in driving the implementation of required changes
You will be navigating through matrix organization, building bridges across departments in order to understand the end-to-end process and accommodate the needs of different stakeholders
You will drive the change with a very hands-on approach, while at the same time keeping the bigger picture in mind and ensuring proper coordination of basic project management processes
As a process improvement project coordinator, you will stay in close contact with all stakeholders and making sure that they are informed in an appropriate and timely manner
You will ensure that project structure is in place, document the deliverables and action items to manage them properly
You will be responsible for coordinating and supporting various smaller projects that are either part of a bigger project or one that is initiated by the team on the floor
You will manage enhancements and be the first line of support of critical tools and software in Distribution Center daily operation, such as Global Shipping Application
Examples of running and upcoming projects include mezzanine and conveyor system installation, WCS implementation, shipping solution software upgrades, SAP WMS enhancements, Voice Picking system improvements, 3PL setup, Lean initiatives, Global Trade System enhancements, etc.
What You Will Need to Succeed:
You will have experience in the field of process improvement and project management with a supply chain background and will have participated in, or coordinated several process improvement projects previously.
Ideally, you will be familiar with Lean principles and the corresponding toolset, such as the A3 problem-solving method.
You will have a data-driven mindset, and you are capable of analysing and interpreting data to identify opportunities to improve a process and build a business case to support it.
You will be a self-starter, comfortable with taking initiative in order to make things happen and follow through without waiting to be told what to do
You will be comfortable picking up small but critical projects as well as larger long-term enhancements
You will be Tech Savvy and have experience in testing and IT enhancements
Your English language skills are advanced. You feel at home in an international environment and can communicate in a professional way at all levels within, and outside the organization.
You will be educated to Bachelor level or higher
You will have experience in a distribution/warehouse environment
You will have the ability to work with limited supervision
Result-driven and sense of ownership
Excellent excel skills needed for this role
Familiarity with SAP is a plus

We have customers in over 175 countries and a global workforce of over 9,000 talented people.

So, what does that mean for you? We enrich the livelihoods of our employees with a positive and respectful work culture that embraces challenges and encourages learning and discovery. 67,supply,Indeed,p_a7947e077c0f49ca,Process Improvement Project Coordinator,IDEXX, Hoofddorp,"Our Distribution and Instrument Service center is looking for a Process Improvement Project Coordinator to continue supporting the rapid growth of our organization. Seated in Hoofddorp (Amsterdam area), which is our international headquarter location, we are on the center stage of our operations in the EMEA and APO region. This is an outstanding opportunity to be part of our international operations team of a growing biotech company that was recently added to the S&P 500 and the NASDAQ 100 Index!
The purpose of this very versatile role is to support the Supply Chain operations team with the increasing volume of project-related work driven by the growth of the organization. You will participate in and / or lead small and large initiatives and projects. Depending on the situation, you will be responsible for either the organizational and planning aspects, or the execution, or both.
In this Role:
You will be supporting continuous improvement in the Supply Chain organization, analysing and evaluating processes, proactively coming up with improvement recommendations
You will be building a solid business case using a problem-solving method and data analysis and taking an active role in driving the implementation of required changes
You will be navigating through matrix organization, building bridges across departments in order to understand the end-to-end process and accommodate the needs of different stakeholders
You will drive the change with a very hands-on approach, while at the same time keeping the bigger picture in mind and ensuring proper coordination of basic project management processes
As a process improvement project coordinator, you will stay in close contact with all stakeholders and making sure that they are informed in an appropriate and timely manner
You will ensure that project structure is in place, document the deliverables and action items to manage them properly
You will be responsible for coordinating and supporting various smaller projects that are either part of a bigger project or one that is initiated by the team on the floor
You will manage enhancements and be the first line of support of critical tools and software in Distribution Center daily operation, such as Global Shipping Application
Examples of running and upcoming projects include mezzanine and conveyor system installation, WCS implementation, shipping solution software upgrades, SAP WMS enhancements, Voice Picking system improvements, 3PL setup, Lean initiatives, Global Trade System enhancements, etc.
What You Will Need to Succeed:
You will have experience in the field of process improvement and project management with a supply chain background and will have participated in, or coordinated several process improvement projects previously.
Ideally, you will be familiar with Lean principles and the corresponding toolset, such as the A3 problem-solving method.
You will have a data-driven mindset, and you are capable of analysing and interpreting data to identify opportunities to improve a process and build a business case to support it.
You will be a self-starter, comfortable with taking initiative in order to make things happen and follow through without waiting to be told what to do
You will be comfortable picking up small but critical projects as well as larger long-term enhancements
You will be Tech Savvy and have experience in testing and IT enhancements
Your English language skills are advanced. You feel at home in an international environment and can communicate in a professional way at all levels within, and outside the organization.
You will be educated to Bachelor level or higher
You will have experience in a distribution/warehouse environment
You will have the ability to work with limited supervision
Result-driven and sense of ownership
Excellent excel skills needed for this role
Familiarity with SAP is a plus

73,supply,Indeed,p_fd2375f9ac3f9358,Process Improvement Project Coordinator,IDEXX, Hoofddorp,"Our Distribution and Instrument Service center is looking for a Process Improvement Project Coordinator to continue supporting the rapid growth of our organization. Seated in Hoofddorp (Amsterdam area), which is our international headquarter location, we are on the center stage of our operations in the EMEA and APO region. This is an outstanding opportunity to be part of our international operations team of a growing biotech company that was recently added to the S&P 500 and the NASDAQ 100 Index!
The purpose of this very versatile role is to support the Supply Chain operations team with the increasing volume of project-related work driven by the growth of the organization. You will participate in and / or lead small and large initiatives and projects. Depending on the situation, you will be responsible for either the organizational and planning aspects, or the execution, or both.
In this Role:
You will be supporting continuous improvement in the Supply Chain organization, analysing and evaluating processes, proactively coming up with improvement recommendations
You will be building a solid business case using a problem-solving method and data analysis and taking an active role in driving the implementation of required changes
You will be navigating through matrix organization, building bridges across departments in order to understand the end-to-end process and accommodate the needs of different stakeholders
You will drive the change with a very hands-on approach, while at the same time keeping the bigger picture in mind and ensuring proper coordination of basic project management processes
As a process improvement project coordinator, you will stay in close contact with all stakeholders and making sure that they are informed in an appropriate and timely manner
You will ensure that project structure is in place, document the deliverables and action items to manage them properly
You will be responsible for coordinating and supporting various smaller projects that are either part of a bigger project or one that is initiated by the team on the floor
You will manage enhancements and be the first line of support of critical tools and software in Distribution Center daily operation, such as Global Shipping Application
Examples of running and upcoming projects include mezzanine and conveyor system installation, WCS implementation, shipping solution software upgrades, SAP WMS enhancements, Voice Picking system improvements, 3PL setup, Lean initiatives, Global Trade System enhancements, etc.
What You Will Need to Succeed:
You will have experience in the field of process improvement and project management with a supply chain background and will have participated in, or coordinated several process improvement projects previously.
Ideally, you will be familiar with Lean principles and the corresponding toolset, such as the A3 problem-solving method.
You will have a data-driven mindset, and you are capable of analysing and interpreting data to identify opportunities to improve a process and build a business case to support it.
You will be a self-starter, comfortable with taking initiative in order to make things happen and follow through without waiting to be told what to do
You will be comfortable picking up small but critical projects as well as larger long-term enhancements
You will be Tech Savvy and have experience in testing and IT enhancements
Your English language skills are advanced. You feel at home in an international environment and can communicate in a professional way at all levels within, and outside the organization.
You will be educated to Bachelor level or higher
You will have experience in a distribution/warehouse environment
You will have the ability to work with limited supervision
Result-driven and sense of ownership
Excellent excel skills needed for this role
Familiarity with SAP is a plus

Depending on the situation, you will be responsible for either the organizational and planning aspects, or the execution, or both.
In this Role:
You will be supporting continuous improvement in the Supply Chain organization, analysing and evaluating processes, proactively coming up with improvement recommendations
You will be building a solid business case using a problem-solving method and data analysis and taking an active role in driving the implementation of required changes
You will be navigating through matrix organization, building bridges across departments in order to understand the end-to-end process and accommodate the needs of different stakeholders
You will drive the change with a very hands-on approach, while at the same time keeping the bigger picture in mind and ensuring proper coordination of basic project management processes
As a process improvement project coordinator, you will stay in close contact with all stakeholders and making sure that they are informed in an appropriate and timely manner
You will ensure that project structure is in place, document the deliverables and action items to manage them properly
You will be responsible for coordinating and supporting various smaller projects that are either part of a bigger project or one that is initiated by the team on the floor
You will manage enhancements and be the first line of support of critical tools and software in Distribution Center daily operation, such as Global Shipping Application
Examples of running and upcoming projects include mezzanine and conveyor system installation, WCS implementation, shipping solution software upgrades, SAP WMS enhancements, Voice Picking system improvements, 3PL setup, Lean initiatives, Global Trade System enhancements, etc.
What You Will Need to Succeed:
You will have experience in the field of process improvement and project management with a supply chain background and will have participated in, or coordinated several process improvement projects previously.
Ideally, you will be familiar with Lean principles and the corresponding toolset, such as the A3 problem-solving method.
You will have a data-driven mindset, and you are capable of analysing and interpreting data to identify opportunities to improve a process and build a business case to support it.
You will be a self-starter, comfortable with taking initiative in order to make things happen and follow through without waiting to be told what to do
You will be comfortable picking up small but critical projects as well as larger long-term enhancements
You will be Tech Savvy and have experience in testing and IT enhancements
Your English language skills are advanced. You feel at home in an international environment and can communicate in a professional way at all levels within, and outside the organization.
You will be educated to Bachelor level or higher
You will have experience in a distribution/warehouse environment
You will have the ability to work with limited supervision
Result-driven and sense of ownership
Excellent excel skills needed for this role
Familiarity with SAP is a plus
Why IDEXX
We’re proud of the work we do, because our work matters. An innovation leader in every industry we serve, we follow our Purpose and Guiding Principles to help pet owners worldwide keep their companion animals healthy and happy, to ensure safe drinking water for billions, and to help farmers protect livestock and poultry from diseases. We have customers in over 175 countries and a global workforce of over 9,000 talented people.

So, what does that mean for you? We enrich the livelihoods of our employees with a positive and respectful work culture that embraces challenges and encourages learning and discovery. At IDEXX, you will be supported by competitive compensation, incentives, and benefits while enjoying purposeful work that drives improvement.

Let’s pursue what matters together.

We are looking for an experienced biofuel feedstock trader with expertise in the sourcing and trade of used cooking oil (UCO) and tallow (animal fats including Poultry Fat, Beef Tallow, Choice White Grease, etc). Experience in vegetable oils, like soybean oil, canola oil, or distiller’s corn oil is considered an asset. The feedstock traded will be used to produce Biodiesel and Renewable Diesel Fuel (HVO). Relevant experience includes domestic North American origination and sales, as well as international trade (imports and exports).
Responsibilities
Working in your location as part of our International Feedstock Trading Desk based in Boston, MA, USA.
Working closely with Targray’s existing biodiesel trading teams in North America and Europe, as well as Targray’s Global Vegoil desk in Geneva.
Collaborating with Targray’s Risk and Senior Management teams
Developing new trading opportunities and supply sources across Europe
Cultivating and maintaining relationships with suppliers and end users.
Collaborating closely with the operations and logistics team to ensure smooth and timely trades
Monitoring market trends to capitalize on trading opportunities
Requirements
Proven track record of profitable trading in the biofuel feedstock sector
3+ years’ experience in feedstock trading. (UCO / animal tallow / vegetable oil)
Strong existing network of relevant contacts including producers and end-users
Ability to effectively collaborate with team members on a remote basis
Employment Benefits
Generous company-wide profit-sharing plan
Medical and dental insurance
Free access to private healthcare providers for medical emergencies
Retirement Savings Plan w/ employer matching
Targray offers flexibility in terms of the location of the trading desk
Targray provides a highly-competitive remuneration plan and an excellent working environment in a growing multinational firm focused on creating a more sustainable global economy. For more information about our company, please visit https://www.targray.com/

93,supply,Indeed,p_dc83196386ddc6a4,Supply Chain Manager (Pharma),myTomorrows, Amsterdam,"The task of facilitating access to treatment for patients with an unmet medical need involves gathering together individuals from a wide range of pharma, medical, tech and business-oriented fields. In this incredibly dynamic environment, we are looking for a team player with the same values, right skill set and motivation.
Our ideal candidate is an intrinsically motivated professional who enjoys getting things done while navigating the complex global landscapes of Expanded Access.

As Supply Chain Manager, you will be responsible for global supply management on a day to day basis; maintaining system integrity and overseeing operations, dispatch, ordering, warehousing and on-time delivery in compliance with GDP and GMP.

You will also represent the company’s Supply Chain Operations as subject matter expert in discussions with potential clients (pharmaceutical companies) and logistics service providers. You will work closely together with our Supply Chain Officer, who will report into you.

On top of this, we have started a project to replace our current order and product database. In your role, you will be key in this very important project to improve and scale-up myTomorrows’ business.

As our end customers are patients with an unmet need, you need a sense of urgency and the ability to make rapid, disciplined decisions. Overseeing projects of varying size and scope as well as managing smaller more detailed processes, should both appeal to you. We expect you to recommend new initiatives and improve and optimize current supply processes; closely working together with Medical Affairs, Quality, Regulatory Affairs and Project Management.
Your key-responsibilities:

Take ownership of the ordering process and carry out activities, starting from order receipt until the delivery at the customer. Troubleshoot problems in the supply chain procedures and takes responsibility of the on-time delivery of the product at the customer.
Responsible for selection of shipment configurations, means of control for each shipment route.
Manage and maintain product and order databases.
Accurate stock control for different regions and (re)ordering products, taking into account market forecasts, shelf life of the product and legal requirements.
Ensure supply chain procedures are effectively executed and in line with GDP and GMP.
Oversee and manage logistics service providers performing activities on behalf of myTomorrows.
Responsible for selection and qualification of (new) Logistic Service Providers (together with Quality Unit).
Investigate and propose strategy for further global expansion.
Maintain internal country intelligence on import requirements and ensure compliance.
Act as supply chain subject matter expert (SME) in- and outside the myTomorrows organization.
Participate in (internal) audits and inspections.
Select (and implement) new order database.
A health, life science or medical science degree or equivalent by education or experience.
4+ years of (Global) Supply Chain Management experience in the pharmaceutical industry.
Thorough knowledge of Global/European supply chain requirements.
Knowledgeable on drug development and regulatory aspects.
Strong communication and time management skills; have the ability to work independently with minimal supervision.
Rational approach to issues and their business implications, good problem solving and decision-making skills.
Ability to analyze problems, identify, recommend and negotiate alternative solutions and think along with clients (relationship building skills with clients).
Excellent verbal and written communication skills and an ability to work cross functionally at all levels (fluent in English).
The ability to collaborate with other departments to ensure a smooth process and work constructively.
Who we are

myTomorrows is an Amsterdam-based health-tech company specialized in pre-approval access. We help patients with an unmet medical need discover, find and access treatments in development. We are determined to solve the extremely complex puzzle of equitably connecting as many patients as possible with innovations in medicine.

Over the last seven years myTomorrows has helped more than 5,000 patients around the world and has partnered with over 30 pharma and biotech companies to facilitate access to treatment. With offices in Amsterdam and New York City, our team is as diverse as our patient base and we’re excited to continue offering a product and service that makes a difference globally. At myTomorrows wherever you are, whichever role you play, you’re guaranteed to share your day with committed, inspired, and resourceful teammates.
myTomorrows is an Equal Opportunity Employer and, beyond upholding discrimination-free practices, we are committed to cultivating a workplace where difference and diversity are protected and celebrated.

94,supply,Indeed,p_8628e9b9aae7d457,Supply Chain Manager (Pharma),myTomorrows, Amsterdam,"The task of facilitating access to treatment for patients with an unmet medical need involves gathering together individuals from a wide range of pharma, medical, tech and business-oriented fields. In this incredibly dynamic environment, we are looking for a team player with the same values, right skill set and motivation.
Our ideal candidate is an intrinsically motivated professional who enjoys getting things done while navigating the complex global landscapes of Expanded Access.

As Supply Chain Manager, you will be responsible for global supply management on a day to day basis; maintaining system integrity and overseeing operations, dispatch, ordering, warehousing and on-time delivery in compliance with GDP and GMP.

You will also represent the company’s Supply Chain Operations as subject matter expert in discussions with potential clients (pharmaceutical companies) and logistics service providers. You will work closely together with our Supply Chain Officer, who will report into you.

On top of this, we have started a project to replace our current order and product database. In your role, you will be key in this very important project to improve and scale-up myTomorrows’ business.

As our end customers are patients with an unmet need, you need a sense of urgency and the ability to make rapid, disciplined decisions. Overseeing projects of varying size and scope as well as managing smaller more detailed processes, should both appeal to you. We expect you to recommend new initiatives and improve and optimize current supply processes; closely working together with Medical Affairs, Quality, Regulatory Affairs and Project Management.
Your key-responsibilities:

Take ownership of the ordering process and carry out activities, starting from order receipt until the delivery at the customer. Troubleshoot problems in the supply chain procedures and takes responsibility of the on-time delivery of the product at the customer.
Responsible for selection of shipment configurations, means of control for each shipment route.
Manage and maintain product and order databases.
Accurate stock control for different regions and (re)ordering products, taking into account market forecasts, shelf life of the product and legal requirements.
Ensure supply chain procedures are effectively executed and in line with GDP and GMP.
Oversee and manage logistics service providers performing activities on behalf of myTomorrows.
Responsible for selection and qualification of (new) Logistic Service Providers (together with Quality Unit).
Investigate and propose strategy for further global expansion.
Maintain internal country intelligence on import requirements and ensure compliance.
Act as supply chain subject matter expert (SME) in- and outside the myTomorrows organization.
Participate in (internal) audits and inspections.
Select (and implement) new order database.
A health, life science or medical science degree or equivalent by education or experience.
4+ years of (Global) Supply Chain Management experience in the pharmaceutical industry.
Thorough knowledge of Global/European supply chain requirements.
Knowledgeable on drug development and regulatory aspects.
Strong communication and time management skills; have the ability to work independently with minimal supervision.
Rational approach to issues and their business implications, good problem solving and decision-making skills.
Ability to analyze problems, identify, recommend and negotiate alternative solutions and think along with clients (relationship building skills with clients).
Excellent verbal and written communication skills and an ability to work cross functionally at all levels (fluent in English).
The ability to collaborate with other departments to ensure a smooth process and work constructively.
Who we are

myTomorrows is an Amsterdam-based health-tech company specialized in pre-approval access. We help patients with an unmet medical need discover, find and access treatments in development. We are determined to solve the extremely complex puzzle of equitably connecting as many patients as possible with innovations in medicine.

Over the last seven years myTomorrows has helped more than 5,000 patients around the world and has partnered with over 30 pharma and biotech companies to facilitate access to treatment. With offices in Amsterdam and New York City, our team is as diverse as our patient base and we’re excited to continue offering a product and service that makes a difference globally. As Supply Chain Manager, you will be responsible for global supply management on a day to day basis; maintaining system integrity and overseeing operations, dispatch, ordering, warehousing and on-time delivery in compliance with GDP and GMP.

You will also represent the company’s Supply Chain Operations as subject matter expert in discussions with potential clients (pharmaceutical companies) and logistics service providers. You will work closely together with our Supply Chain Officer, who will report into you.

On top of this, we have started a project to replace our current order and product database. In your role, you will be key in this very important project to improve and scale-up myTomorrows’ business.

As our end customers are patients with an unmet need, you need a sense of urgency and the ability to make rapid, disciplined decisions. Overseeing projects of varying size and scope as well as managing smaller more detailed processes, should both appeal to you. We expect you to recommend new initiatives and improve and optimize current supply processes; closely working together with Medical Affairs, Quality, Regulatory Affairs and Project Management.
Your key-responsibilities:

Take ownership of the ordering process and carry out activities, starting from order receipt until the delivery at the customer. Troubleshoot problems in the supply chain procedures and takes responsibility of the on-time delivery of the product at the customer.
Responsible for selection of shipment configurations, means of control for each shipment route.
Manage and maintain product and order databases.
Accurate stock control for different regions and (re)ordering products, taking into account market forecasts, shelf life of the product and legal requirements.
Ensure supply chain procedures are effectively executed and in line with GDP and GMP.
Oversee and manage logistics service providers performing activities on behalf of myTomorrows.
Responsible for selection and qualification of (new) Logistic Service Providers (together with Quality Unit).
Investigate and propose strategy for further global expansion.
Maintain internal country intelligence on import requirements and ensure compliance.
Act as supply chain subject matter expert (SME) in- and outside the myTomorrows organization.
Participate in (internal) audits and inspections.
Select (and implement) new order database.
A health, life science or medical science degree or equivalent by education or experience.
4+ years of (Global) Supply Chain Management experience in the pharmaceutical industry.
Thorough knowledge of Global/European supply chain requirements.
Knowledgeable on drug development and regulatory aspects.
Strong communication and time management skills; have the ability to work independently with minimal supervision.
Rational approach to issues and their business implications, good problem solving and decision-making skills.
Ability to analyze problems, identify, recommend and negotiate alternative solutions and think along with clients (relationship building skills with clients).
Excellent verbal and written communication skills and an ability to work cross functionally at all levels (fluent in English).
The ability to collaborate with other departments to ensure a smooth process and work constructively.
Who we are

myTomorrows is an Amsterdam-based health-tech company specialized in pre-approval access. We help patients with an unmet medical need discover, find and access treatments in development. We are determined to solve the extremely complex puzzle of equitably connecting as many patients as possible with innovations in medicine.

Over the last seven years myTomorrows has helped more than 5,000 patients around the world and has partnered with over 30 pharma and biotech companies to facilitate access to treatment. With offices in Amsterdam and New York City, our team is as diverse as our patient base and we’re excited to continue offering a product and service that makes a difference globally. At myTomorrows wherever you are, whichever role you play, you’re guaranteed to share your day with committed, inspired, and resourceful teammates.
myTomorrows is an Equal Opportunity Employer and, beyond upholding discrimination-free practices, we are committed to cultivating a workplace where difference and diversity are protected and celebrated.

JOB PURPOSE AND IMPACT

The Sustainability Assurance lead is responsible for the company’s systems, processes and procedures necessary to comply with a portfolio of assigned sustainability programs, ranging from regulated government programs to voluntary certification schemes for global or regional. In this role, you will be the subject matter authority and regional lead. In coordination with additional businesses and functions, you will design and deliver a robust compliance monitoring system effectively embedding compliance activities into the regional or local sourcing and logistics organization and within our supplier base.

KEY ACCOUNTABILITIES

Lead the design and implementation of specific internal capabilities, systems, processes and protocols required to ensure compliance with program standards, policies and regulations and meet customer needs.
Promote sustainability compliance, and be at the forefront of building a high performance, quality culture including setting and meeting clear and decisive goals aligned to business strategies, budget management and controls.
Develop and implement a robust due diligence management system by Identifying risks areas and leading the implement and assure the connectivity and collaboration within the company.
Provide expertise in sustainability program standards, collaborating with the commercial, supply chain and finance teams, to mitigate risks and support the embedding of the certification standard compliance management systems in the region.
Ensure program compliance by leading internal audits for defined areas, including defining and prioritizing audit plans based on risk evaluations, establishing an audit, conducting field audits, submitting audit reports, presenting audit findings and ensuring corrective actions are fulfilled.
Identify trends, engaging with external stakeholder and keeping program knowledge current as regulations change over time to identify potential business impact.
Independently handle complex issues with minimal supervision, while escalating only the most complex issues to appropriate staff.
Other duties as assigned

MINIMUM QUALIFICATIONS

Bachelor’s degree in a related field or equivalent experience
Minimum of four years of related work experience

PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS

Seven years of working experience in compliance, quality or sustainability assurance domain
Experience developing and implementing compliance systems, change management and due diligence management processes and procedures.
Experience working at a high level within audit and assurance, focused on environmental and social issues
Verifiable experience of managing sustainability and supply chain transparency programs through standards and assurance.

108,supply,Indeed,p_d794d51bcc296200,Sustainability Assurance lead,Cargill, Schiphol,"Want to build a stronger, more sustainable future and cultivate your career? Join Cargill's global team of 155,000 employees who are committed to safe, responsible and sustainable ways to nourish the world. This position is in Cargill’s food ingredients and bio-industrial business, where we anticipate trends around taste, nutrition and safety to innovate and provide solutions to manufacturers, retailers and foodservice companies.

JOB PURPOSE AND IMPACT

The Sustainability Assurance lead is responsible for the company’s systems, processes and procedures necessary to comply with a portfolio of assigned sustainability programs, ranging from regulated government programs to voluntary certification schemes for global or regional. In this role, you will be the subject matter authority and regional lead. In coordination with additional businesses and functions, you will design and deliver a robust compliance monitoring system effectively embedding compliance activities into the regional or local sourcing and logistics organization and within our supplier base.

KEY ACCOUNTABILITIES

Lead the design and implementation of specific internal capabilities, systems, processes and protocols required to ensure compliance with program standards, policies and regulations and meet customer needs.
Promote sustainability compliance, and be at the forefront of building a high performance, quality culture including setting and meeting clear and decisive goals aligned to business strategies, budget management and controls.
Develop and implement a robust due diligence management system by Identifying risks areas and leading the implement and assure the connectivity and collaboration within the company.
Provide expertise in sustainability program standards, collaborating with the commercial, supply chain and finance teams, to mitigate risks and support the embedding of the certification standard compliance management systems in the region.
Ensure program compliance by leading internal audits for defined areas, including defining and prioritizing audit plans based on risk evaluations, establishing an audit, conducting field audits, submitting audit reports, presenting audit findings and ensuring corrective actions are fulfilled.
Identify trends, engaging with external stakeholder and keeping program knowledge current as regulations change over time to identify potential business impact.
Independently handle complex issues with minimal supervision, while escalating only the most complex issues to appropriate staff.
Other duties as assigned

MINIMUM QUALIFICATIONS

Bachelor’s degree in a related field or equivalent experience
Minimum of four years of related work experience

PREFERRED QUALIFICATIONS

Seven years of working experience in compliance, quality or sustainability assurance domain
Experience developing and implementing compliance systems, change management and due diligence management processes and procedures.
Experience working at a high level within audit and assurance, focused on environmental and social issues
Verifiable experience of managing sustainability and supply chain transparency programs through standards and assurance.
Knowledge of quality, sustainability assurance or regulatory compliance domain / working field is preferred, sustainability knowledge is a pre

116,supply,Indeed,p_f07f767a1d3fc209,General Manager Business Unit Nutrition & Coffee,Trivium Packaging, Schiphol,"Trivium Packaging is a global leader in metal packaging with more than 60 locations worldwide, nearly 8,000 employees, and an annual revenue of approximately $3 billion. Trivium serves a diverse range of customers in a variety of end markets such as food, seafood, pet food, nutrition, beauty and personal care, household care, and premium beverages.

Trivium wants to shape the industry and has embarked on an ambitious transformation journey. In the near term, focus is on building & upskilling the team, deciding where to play & how to win, and increasing financial performance by executing the Trivium Business System (commercial, operational, and supply chain excellence). In addition, Trivium has ambitious sustainability targets and focuses exclusively on products that are infinitely recyclable.

The global head office is at the World Trade Center at Amsterdam Airport, however many people work in virtual teams from different countries. The culture is results-driven, entrepreneurial, informal, and highly multicultural. Young people have a high degree of responsibility.

The GM BU Nutrion & Coffee acts as General Manager/’CEO’ of a Trivium Business Unit (EUR >300 M revenue, >850 employees, 5 plants (3 in NL, 1 in DK, 1 in GE) with full P&L responsibility. The GM BU Nutrion & Coffee reports (solid) line to the President of the European Division and has direct control over all BU related resources respectively P&L except centrally procured (bundling effect) key materials such as tinplate, aluminum, energy and lacquers. The BU GM N&C collaborates the Global Key Account Organization and Group Procurement.

Key Responsibilities

Safety: Drives proactively safety and risk mitigation, directly leads the BU H&S manager.
Is a role model of Trivium's values and leadership behaviors, represents Trivium and the Business Unit as primary point of contact for internal (employees, BU/Division/Group Management) and external stakeholders (Local authorities, local community incl. plant neighbors, interested job applicants, customer visits, customer audits, etc.)
Owns, communicates, and cascades Trivium’s (Business Unit) strategy into specific actions that the employees can understand and act on; Assigns individual implementation responsibilities, monitors and executes (implementation controlling), ensures quality of results, and provides 'upward' feedback.""
Collaborates with other Trivium BU GMs to align on Business Unit-overarching topics (e.g., foot print optimization, bundling of component production, etc.) and to exchange best practices
Builds and motivates a successful team that drives performance and embodies the Trivium values
Creates a strong performance management culture, recognizing achievements and quickly acting on consequences
Assess the current team's capabilities against role expectations. Build the team's capabilities to be able to grow into future roles. Ensures succession for key roles, collaborates with HR on succession plan
Understands and acts on OHI feedback (employee survey feedback) and drives actions to increase ownership of all employees in the plant
Acts together with HR as primary contact for the local works council
Ensures that financial and nonfinancial BU, BU-sales, and BU plant results are meeting or exceeding agreed on commitments and steers plant controller on proper reporting on it.
Owns and manages the BU P&L – from sales to BU-EBIT(DA); defines and monitors actions to achieve yearly budget targets (adjusted for plant allocations where relevant)
Ensures that lean operations (OpEx project) are implemented and ensures savings can be achieved
Collaborates with Group procurement to capture procurement savings
Supports SG&A cost reductions and company-wide initiatives, where applicable to the plant
Plans and executes plant CAPEX and restructuring (RCO) projects on time and within budget
Acts as role model, sparring partner, and back-up for BU safety manager, BU SCM manager, and BU head of quality
Governs SCM as linking pin between sales (orders) and production, decides quickly tradeoffs in the overall Trivium interest
Work with commercial team to quickly resolve any issues from external and internal customers, organizes and hosts customer visits and customer audits in plant
Organizes and continuously improves a smooth production flow, increasing overall asset utilization, limited WIP/material and semifinished inventory, minimum number of changeovers/set-ups and high OTIF (>99%)
Quality: Prioritizes a do-it-right-first-time quality culture over spoilage, cost, profitability and minimizes the complaints from customers.
Collaborates with R&D, OSG (Process Expert Team), and Operational Excellence on product and process innovation, continuous improvement, product complexity reduction, and stock management

Education & Training

Application
